<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bonobo.html>bonobo</a> (94985)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> Bolobo, <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:village.html>village</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:on.html>on</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:congo.html>Congo</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:river.html>River</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:where.html>where</a> Europeans <a href = vnd.unilang:first.html>first</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:made.html>made</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:contact.html>contact</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:species.html>species</a>. Bolobo <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:possibly.html>possibly</a> imitative <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> bubbling <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> rapids <a href = vnd.unilang:at.html>at</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:that.html>that</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:section.html>section</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:congo.html>Congo</a>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***bonze.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bonze.html>bonze</a> (132926)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Japanese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Japanese language">Japanese</a></span> <i class="Jpan mention" lang="ja">凡僧</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>The</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sense.html>sense</a> “bigwig” derives <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:bonze.html>Bonze</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p>17th <a href = vnd.unilang:century.html>century</a>. <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language"><a href = vnd.unilang:spanish.html>Spanish</a></a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es"><a href = vnd.unilang:bobo.html>bobo</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">balbus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stammering</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***boom.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:boom.html>boom</a> (1312)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bôom</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">bōm</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*baumaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boom.html>boom</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bomen.html>bomen</a></b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boompje.html>boompje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:tree.html>tree</a></li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:any.html>any</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:solid.html>solid</a>, pole-shaped, <a href = vnd.unilang:usually.html>usually</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wooden.html>wooden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:object.html>object</a>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:beam.html>beam</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mast.html>mast</a></span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mast.html>mast</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language"><a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:boom.html>boom</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>A</a> raised <a href = vnd.unilang:platform.html>platform</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:often.html>often</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:flight.html>flight</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:steps.html>steps</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:that.html>that</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lead.html>lead</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:into.html>into</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:building.html>building</a></li>

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:borgen.html>borgen</a></i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:equivalent.html>Equivalent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:borg.html>borg</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.

</p>
